.{created_ids.items.len});\n   224→    }\n   225→}\n   226→\n   227→/// Run the import command.\n   228→/// Imports issues from a JSONL file with single lock acquisition.\n   229→pub fn runImport(\n return BatchError.FileReadError;\n   263→    };\n   264→    defer {\n   265→        for (imported_issues.issues) |*issue| {\n   266→            var i = issue.*;\n   267→ allocator.free(imported_issues.corrupt_lines);\n   272→        }\n   273→    }\n   274→\n   275→    if (import_args.dry_run) {\n   276→        // Dry run - just report what would be imported\n   277→        if (structured_output) {\n   278→            try output.printJson(ImportResult{\n   279→                .success = true,\n   280→                .issues_imported = imported_issues.issues.len,\n (!global.quiet) {\n   285→            try output.info(\"Would import {d} issue(s), skip {d} corrupt entries\", .{\n   286→                imported_issues.issues.len,\n   287→                imported_issues.corruption_count,\n   288→            });\n   289→        }\n   290→        return;\n   291→    }\n   292→\n   293→    // Load existing issues\n   294→    var store = try common.outputErrorTyped(ImportResult, &output, structured_output, \"failed to load existing issues\");\n   300→            return BatchError.StorageError;\n   301→        }\n   302→    };\n   303→\n   304→    var imported_count: usize = 0;\n   305→    var skipped_count: usize = 0;\n   306→    var updated_count: usize = 0;\n   307→\n   308→    const now = std.time.timestamp();\n   309→\n   310→    for (imported_issues.issues) |issue| {\n   311→        if (import_args.merge) {\n   312→            // Merge mode: update if exists, insert if not\n   313→            if (try store.exists(issue.id)) {\n   314→                // Update existing issue\n   315→                store.update(issue.id, .{\n   316→                    .title = issue.title,\n   317→                    .description = issue.description,\n   318→                    .status = issue.status,\n   319→                    .priority = issue.priority,\n   320→                    .issue_type = continue;\n   325→                };\n   326→                updated_count += 1;\n   327→            } else {\n   328→                store.insert(issue) catch {\n   329→                    skipped_count += 1;\n   330→                    continue;\n   331→                };\n   332→                imported_count += 1;\n   333→            }\n   334→        } else {\n   335→            // Replace mode: skip if exists\n   336→            if (try store.exists(issue.id)) {\n   337→                skipped_count += 1;\n   338→                continue;\n   339→            }\n   340→            store.insert(issue) catch {\n   341→                skipped_count += 1;\n   342→                continue;\n   343→            };\n   344→            imported_count += 1;\n   345→        }\n   346→    }\n   347→\n   348→    // Single atomic save\n   349→    if (!global.no_auto_flush) {\n   350→        store.saveToFile() catch {\n   351→            try common.outputErrorTyped(ImportResult, &output, structured_output, \"failed to save issues\");\n   352→            return BatchError.StorageError;\n   353→        };\n   354→    }\n   355→\n   356→    // Output result\n   357→    if (structured_output) {\n   358→        try output.printJson(ImportResult{\n   359→            .success = true,\n   360→            .issues_imported = imported_count,\n   361→            .issues_updated = if (import_args.merge) updated_count else null,\n   362→            .issues_skipped = skipped_count + imported_issues.corruption_count,\n   363→        });\n   364→    } else if (!global.quiet) {\n   365→        if (import_args.merge and updated_count > 0) {\n   366→            try output.success(\"Imported {d}, updated {d}, skipped {d} issue(s)\", .{\n   367→                imported_count,\n   368→                updated_count,\n   369→                skipped_count,\n   370→            });\n   371→        } else {\n   372→            try output.success(\"Imported {d}, skipped {d} issue(s)\", .{ imported_count, skipped_count });\n   373→        }\n   374→    }\n   375→}\n   376→\n   377→/// Read file content into a buffer.\n   378→fn readFileContent(path: []const u8, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) ![]u8 {\n   379→    const file = try std.fs.cwd().openFile(path, .{});\n   380→    defer file.close();\n   381→    return try file.readToEndAlloc(allocator, 100 * 1024 * 1024); // 100MB max\n   382→}\n   383→\n   384→\n   385→/// Check if a file contains git merge conflict markers.\n   386→fn hasMergeConflicts(path: []const u8, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) !bool {\n   387→    const file = std.fs.cwd().openFile(path, .{}) catch |err| switch (err) {\n   388→        error.FileNotFound => return false,\n   389→        else => return err,\n   390→    };\n   391→    defer file.close();\n   392→\n   393→    const content = try file.readToEndAlloc(allocator, 1024 * 1024 * 10);\n   394→    defer allocator.free(content);\n   395→\n   396→    if (std.mem.indexOf(u8, content, \"<<<<<<<\") != null) return true;\n   397→    if (std.mem.indexOf(u8, content, \"=======\") != null) return true;\n   398→    if (std.mem.indexOf(u8, content, \">>>>>>>\") != null) return true;\n   399→\n   400→    return false;\n   401→}\n   402→\n   403→/// Get the default actor name from environment.\n   404→fn getDefaultActor() ?[]const u8 {\n   405→    const builtin = @import(\"builtin\");\n   406→    if (builtin.os.tag == .windows) return null;\n   407→    return std.posix.getenv(\"USER\") orelse std.posix.getenv(\"USERNAME\");\n   408→}\n   409→\n   410→/// Read Batch operations for beads_zig.\n//!\n//! - `bz add-batch` - Create multiple issues from stdin/file with single lock\n//! - `bz import <file>` - Import issues from JSONL file with single lock\n//!\n//! These operations reduce lock contention for bulk operations by acquiring\n//! a single lock, performing all insertions, and releasing.\n\nconst std = @import(\"std\");\nconst models = @import(\"../models/mod.zig\");\nconst storage = @import(\"../storage/mod.zig\");\nconst id_gen = @import(\"../id/mod.zig\");\nconst common = @import(\"common.zig\");\nconst args = @import(\"args.zig\");\nconst test_util = @import(\"../test_util.zig\");\n\nconst Issue = models.Issue;\nconst Priority = models.Priority;\nconst IssueType = models.IssueType;\nconst IssueStore = storage.IssueStore;\nconst JsonlFile = storage.JsonlFile;\nconst IdGenerator = id_gen.IdGenerator;\n\npub const BatchError = error{\n    WorkspaceNotInitialized,\n    StorageError,\n    InvalidInput,\n    FileReadError,\n    NoIssuesToAdd,\n    OutOfMemory,\n};\n\npub const BatchResult = struct {\n    success: bool,\n    issues_created: ?usize = null,\n    issues_imported: ?usize = null,\n    issues_skipped: ?usize = null,\n    ids: ?[]const []const u8 = null,\n    message: ?[]const u8 = null,\n};\n\npub const ImportResult = struct {\n    success: bool,\n    issues_imported: ?usize = null,\n    issues_skipped: ?usize = null,\n    issues_updated: ?usize = null,\n    message: ?[]const u8 = null,\n};\n\n/// Run the add-batch command.\n/// Creates multiple issues with a single lock acquisition and fsync.\npub fn runAddBatch(\n    batch_args: args.AddBatchArgs,\n    global: args.GlobalOptions,\n    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,\n) !void {\n    var output = common.initOutput(allocator, global);\n    const structured_output = global.isStructuredOutput();\n\n    // Determine workspace path\n    const beads_dir = global.data_path orelse \".beads\";\n    const issues_path = try std.fs.path.join(allocator, &.{ beads_dir, \"issues.jsonl\" });\n    defer allocator.free(issues_path);\n\n    // Check if workspace is initialized\n    std.fs.cwd().access(issues_path, .{}) catch |err| {\n        if (err == error.FileNotFound) {\n            try common.outputErrorTyped(BatchResult, &output, structured_output, \"workspace not initialized. Run 'bz init' first.\");\n            return BatchError.WorkspaceNotInitialized;\n        }\n        try common.outputErrorTyped(BatchResult, &output, structured_output, \"cannot access workspace\");\n        return BatchError.StorageError;\n    };\n\n    // Read input from file\n    const file_path = batch_args.file orelse {\n        try common.outputErrorTyped(BatchResult, &output, structured_output, \"file path required. Use 'bz add-batch <file>' or 'bz add-batch --file <file>'\");\n        return BatchError.InvalidInput;\n    };\n\n    const input_content = readFileContent(file_path, allocator) catch {\n        try common.outputErrorTyped(BatchResult, &output, structured_output, \"failed to read input file\");\n        return BatchError.FileReadError;\n    };\n    defer allocator.free(input_content);\n\n    // Parse input based on format\n    var issues_to_add: std.ArrayListUnmanaged(Issue) = .{};\n    defer {\n        for (issues_to_add.items) |*issue| {\n            issue.deinit(allocator);\n        }\n        issues_to_add.deinit(allocator);\n    }\n\n    // Load existing issues to get count for ID generation\n    var store = IssueStore.init(allocator, issues_path);\n    defer store.deinit();\n\n    store.loadFromFile() catch |err| {\n        if (err != error.FileNotFound) {\n            try common.outputErrorTyped(BatchResult, &output, structured_output, \"failed to load issues\");\n            return BatchError.StorageError;\n        }\n    };\n\n    // Get config prefix\n    const prefix = try getConfigPrefix(allocator, beads_dir);\n    defer allocator.free(prefix);\n\n    // Get actor\n    const actor = global.actor orelse getDefaultActor();\n\n    const now = std.time.timestamp();\n    var generator = IdGenerator.init(prefix);\n    var issue_count = store.countTotal();\n\n    // Parse input and create issues\n    switch (batch_args.format) {\n        .titles => {\n            var line_iter = std.mem.splitScalar(u8, input_content, '\\n');\n            while (line_iter.next()) |line| {\n                const trimmed = std.mem.trim(u8, line, \" \\t\\r\");\n                if (trimmed.len == 0) continue;\n                if (trimmed.len > 500) continue; // Skip titles that are too long\n\n                const issue_id = try generator.generate(allocator, issue_count);\n                errdefer allocator.free(issue_id);\n                issue_count += 1;\n\n                var issue = Issue.init(issue_id, trimmed, now);\n                issue.created_by = actor;\n\n                // Clone strings for owned storage\n                const cloned = try issue.clone(allocator);\n                allocator.free(issue_id); // clone made its own copy\n                try issues_to_add.append(allocator, cloned);\n            }\n        },\n        .jsonl => {\n            var line_iter = std.mem.splitScalar(u8, input_content, '\\n');\n            while (line_iter.next()) |line| {\n                const trimmed = std.mem.trim(u8, line, \" \\t\\r\");\n                if (trimmed.len == 0) continue;\n\n                // Parse as Issue JSON\n                const parsed = std.json.parseFromSlice(\n                    Issue,\n                    allocator,\n                    trimmed,\n                    .{ .ignore_unknown_fields = true, .allocate = .alloc_always },\n                ) catch continue; // Skip malformed entries\n\n                // If no ID, generate one\n                var issue = parsed.value;\n                if (issue.id.len == 0) {\n                    const new_id = try generator.generate(allocator, issue_count);\n                    allocator.free(issue.id);\n                    issue.id = new_id;\n                    issue_count += 1;\n                }\n\n                try issues_to_add.append(allocator, issue);\n            }\n        },\n    }\n\n    if (issues_to_add.items.len == 0) {\n        if (structured_output) {\n            try output.printJson(BatchResult{\n                .success = true,\n                .issues_created = 0,\n                .message = \"no issues to add\",\n            });\n        } else if (!global.quiet) {\n            try output.info(\"No issues to add\", .{});\n        }\n        return;\n    }\n\n    // Insert all issues (single save at end)\n    var created_ids: std.ArrayListUnmanaged([]const u8) = .{};\n    defer {\n        for (created_ids.items) |id| {\n            allocator.free(id);\n        }\n        created_ids.deinit(allocator);\n    }\n\n    for (issues_to_add.items) |issue| {\n        store.insert(issue) catch |err| switch (err) {\n            error.DuplicateId => continue, // Skip duplicates\n            else => {\n                try common.outputErrorTyped(BatchResult, &output, structured_output, \"failed to insert issue\");\n                return BatchError.StorageError;\n            },\n        };\n        const id_copy = try allocator.dupe(u8, issue.id);\n        try created_ids.append(allocator, id_copy);\n    }\n\n    // Single atomic save\n    if (!global.no_auto_flush) {\n        store.saveToFile() catch {\n            try common.outputErrorTyped(BatchResult, &output, structured_output, \"failed to save issues\");\n            return BatchError.StorageError;\n        };\n    }\n\n    // Output result\n    if (structured_output) {\n        try output.printJson(BatchResult{\n            .success = true,\n            .issues_created = created_ids.items.len,\n            .ids = created_ids.items,\n        });\n    } else if (global.quiet) {\n        for (created_ids.items) |id| {\n            try output.raw(id);\n            try output.raw(\"\\n\");\n        }\n    } else {\n        try output.success(\"Created {d} issue(s)\", .{created_ids.items.len});\n    }\n}\n\n/// Run the import command.\n/// Imports issues from a JSONL file with single lock acquisition.\npub fn runImport(\n    import_args: args.ImportArgs,\n    global: args.GlobalOptions,\n    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,\n) !void {\n    var output = common.initOutput(allocator, global);\n    const structured_output = global.isStructuredOutput();\n\n    // Determine workspace path\n    const beads_dir = global.data_path orelse \".beads\";\n    const issues_path = try std.fs.path.join(allocator, &.{ beads_dir, \"issues.jsonl\" });\n    defer allocator.free(issues_path);\n\n    // Check if workspace is initialized\n    std.fs.cwd().access(issues_path, .{}) catch |err| {\n        if (err == error.FileNotFound) {\n            try common.outputErrorTyped(ImportResult, &output, structured_output, \"workspace not initialized. Run 'bz init' first.\");\n            return BatchError.WorkspaceNotInitialized;\n        }\n        try common.outputErrorTyped(ImportResult, &output, structured_output, \"cannot access workspace\");\n        return BatchError.StorageError;\n    };\n\n    // Check for merge conflict markers in import file\n    if (try hasMergeConflicts(import_args.file, allocator)) {\n        try common.outputErrorTyped(ImportResult, &output, structured_output, \"import file contains merge conflict markers\");\n        return BatchError.InvalidInput;\n    }\n\n    // Read and parse the import file\n    var import_jsonl = JsonlFile.init(import_args.file, allocator);\n    const imported_issues = import_jsonl.readAllWithRecovery() catch {\n        try common.outputErrorTyped(ImportResult, &output, structured_output, \"failed to read import file\");\n        return BatchError.FileReadError;\n    };\n    defer {\n        for (imported_issues.issues) |*issue| {\n            var i = issue.*;\n            i.deinit(allocator);\n        }\n        allocator.free(imported_issues.issues);\n        if (imported_issues.corrupt_lines.len > 0) {\n            allocator.free(imported_issues.corrupt_lines);\n        }\n    }\n\n    if (import_args.dry_run) {\n        // Dry run - just report what would be imported\n        if (structured_output) {\n            try output.printJson(ImportResult{\n                .success = true,\n                .issues_imported = imported_issues.issues.len,\n                .issues_skipped = imported_issues.corruption_count,\n                .message = \"dry run - no changes made\",\n            });\n        } else if (!global.quiet) {\n            try output.info(\"Would import {d} issue(s), skip {d} corrupt entries\", .{\n                imported_issues.issues.len,\n                imported_issues.corruption_count,\n            });\n        }\n        return;\n    }\n\n    // Load existing issues\n    var store = IssueStore.init(allocator, issues_path);\n    defer store.deinit();\n\n    store.loadFromFile() catch |err| {\n        if (err != error.FileNotFound) {\n            try common.outputErrorTyped(ImportResult, &output, structured_output, \"failed to load existing issues\");\n            return BatchError.StorageError;\n        }\n    };\n\n    var imported_count: usize = 0;\n    var skipped_count: usize = 0;\n    var updated_count: usize = 0;\n\n    const now = std.time.timestamp();\n\n    for (imported_issues.issues) |issue| {\n        if (import_args.merge) {\n            // Merge mode: update if exists, insert if not\n            if (try store.exists(issue.id)) {\n                // Update existing issue\n                store.update(issue.id, .{\n                    .title = issue.title,\n                    .description = issue.description,\n                    .status = issue.status,\n                    .priority = issue.priority,\n                    .issue_type = issue.issue_type,\n                    .assignee = issue.assignee,\n                }, now) catch {\n                    skipped_count += 1;\n                    continue;\n                };\n                updated_count += 1;\n            } else {\n                store.insert(issue) catch {\n                    skipped_count += 1;\n                    continue;\n                };\n                imported_count += 1;\n            }\n        } else {\n            // Replace mode: skip if exists\n            if (try store.exists(issue.id)) {\n                skipped_count += 1;\n                continue;\n            }\n            store.insert(issue) catch {\n                skipped_count += 1;\n                continue;\n            };\n            imported_count += 1;\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Single atomic save\n    if (!global.no_auto_flush) {\n        store.saveToFile() catch {\n            try common.outputErrorTyped(ImportResult, &output, structured_output, \"failed to save issues\");\n            return BatchError.StorageError;\n        };\n    }\n\n    // Output result\n    if (structured_output) {\n        try output.printJson(ImportResult{\n            .success = true,\n            .issues_imported = imported_count,\n            .issues_updated = if (import_args.merge) updated_count else null,\n            .issues_skipped = skipped_count + imported_issues.corruption_count,\n        });\n    } else if (!global.quiet) {\n        if (import_args.merge and updated_count > 0) {\n            try output.success(\"Imported {d}, updated {d}, skipped {d} issue(s)\", .{\n                imported_count,\n                updated_count,\n                skipped_count,\n            });\n        } else {\n            try output.success(\"Imported {d}, skipped {d} issue(s)\", .{ imported_count, skipped_count });\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/// Read file content into a buffer.\nfn readFileContent(path: []const u8, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) ![]u8 {\n    const file = try std.fs.cwd().openFile(path, .{});\n    defer file.close();\n    return try file.readToEndAlloc(allocator, 100 * 1024 * 1024); // 100MB max\n}\n\n\n/// Check if a file contains git merge conflict markers.\nfn hasMergeConflicts(path: []const u8, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) !bool {\n    const file = std.fs.cwd().openFile(path, .{}) catch |err| switch (err) {\n        error.FileNotFound => return false,\n        else => return err,\n    };\n    defer file.close();\n\n    const content = try file.readToEndAlloc(allocator, 1024 * 1024 * 10);\n    defer allocator.free(content);\n\n    if (std.mem.indexOf(u8, content, \"<<<<<<<\") != null) return true;\n    if (std.mem.indexOf(u8, content, \"=======\") != null) return true;\n    if (std.mem.indexOf(u8, content, \">>>>>>>\") != null) return true;\n\n    return false;\n}\n\n/// Get the default actor name from environment.\nfn getDefaultActor() ?[]const u8 {\n    const builtin = @import(\"builtin\");\n    if (builtin.os.tag == .windows) return null;\n    return std.posix.getenv(\"USER\") orelse std.posix.getenv(\"USERNAME\");\n}\n\n/// Read the ID prefix from config.yaml, defaulting to \"bd\".\nfn getConfigPrefix(allocator: std.mem.Allocator, beads_dir: []const u8) ![]u8 {\n    const config_path = try std.fs.path.join(allocator, &.{ beads_dir, \"config.yaml\" });\n    defer allocator.free(config_path);\n\n    const file = std.fs.cwd().openFile(config_path, .{}) catch {\n        return try allocator.dupe(u8, \"bd\");\n    };\n    defer file.close();\n\n    const content = file.readToEndAlloc(allocator, 4096) catch {\n        return try allocator.dupe(u8, \"bd\");\n    };\n    defer allocator.free(content);\n\n    if (std.mem.indexOf(u8, content, \"prefix:\")) |prefix_pos| {\n        const after_prefix = content[prefix_pos + 7 ..];\n        var i: usize = 0;\n        while (i < after_prefix.len and (after_prefix[i] == ' ' or after_prefix[i] == '\\t')) {\n            i += 1;\n        }\n\n        if (i < after_prefix.len) {\n            if (after_prefix[i] == '\"') {\n                i += 1;\n                const start = i;\n                while (i < after_prefix.len and after_prefix[i] != '\"' and after_prefix[i] != '\\n') {\n                    i += 1;\n                }\n                if (i > start) {\n                    return try allocator.dupe(u8, after_prefix[start..i]);\n                }\n            } else {\n                const start = i;\n                while (i < after_prefix.len and after_prefix[i] != '\\n' and after_prefix[i] != ' ' and after_prefix[i] != '\\t') {\n                    i += 1;\n                }\n                if (i > start) {\n                    return try allocator.dupe(u8, after_prefix[start..i]);\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    return try allocator.dupe(u8, \"bd\");\n}\n\n// --- Tests ---\n\ntest single lock acquisition and fsync.\npub fn runAddBatch(\n    batch_args: args.AddBatchArgs,\n    global: args.GlobalOptions,\n    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,\n) !void {\n    var output = common.initOutput(allocator, global);\n    const structured_output = global.isStructuredOutput();\n\n    // Determine workspace path\n    const beads_dir = global.data_path orelse \".beads\";\n    const issues_path = try std.fs.path.join(allocator, &.{ beads_dir, \"issues.jsonl\" });\n    defer allocator.free(issues_path);\n\n    // Check if workspace is initialized\n    std.fs.cwd().access(issues_path, .{}) catch |err| {\n        if (err == error.FileNotFound) {\n            try common.outputErrorTyped(BatchResult, &output, structured_output, \"workspace not initialized. Run 'bz init' first.\");\n            return BatchError.WorkspaceNotInitialized;\n        }\n        try common.outputErrorTyped(BatchResult, &output, structured_output, \"cannot access workspace\");\n        return BatchError.StorageError;\n    };\n\n    // Read input from file\n    const file_path = batch_args.file orelse {\n        try common.outputErrorTyped(BatchResult, &output, structured_output, \"file path required.      issues_to_add.deinit(allocator);\n    }\n\n    // Load existing issues to get count for ID generation\n    var store = IssueStore.init(allocator, issues_path);\n    defer store.deinit();\n\n  const actor = global.actor orelse getDefaultActor();\n\n    const now = std.time.timestamp();\n    var generator = IdGenerator.init(prefix);\n    var issue_count = store.countTotal();\n\n    // Parse input and create issues\n    switch (batch_args.format) {\n        .titles => {\n            var line_iter = std.mem.splitScalar(u8, input_content, '\\n');\n            while (line_iter.next()) |line| {\n                const trimmed = std.mem.trim(u8, line, \" \\t\\r\");\n                if (trimmed.len == 0) continue;\n                if (trimmed.len > 500) continue; // Skip titles that are too long\n\n                const issue_id = try generator.generate(allocator, issue_count);\n                errdefer allocator.free(issue_id);\n                issue_count += 1;\n\n                var issue = Issue.init(issue_id, trimmed, now);\n                issue.created_by = actor;\n\n                // Clone strings for owned storage\n                const cloned = try issue.clone(allocator);\n                allocator.free(issue_id); // clone made its own copy\n                try issues_to_add.append(allocator, cloned);\n            }\n        },\n        .jsonl => {\n            var line_iter = std.mem.splitScalar(u8, input_content, '\\n');\n            while (line_iter.next()) |line| {\n                const trimmed = std.mem.trim(u8, line, \" \\t\\r\");\n                if (trimmed.len == 0) continue;\n\n                // Parse as Issue JSON\n                const parsed = std.json.parseFromSlice(\n                    Issue,\n                    allocator,\n                    trimmed,\n                    .{ .ignore_unknown_fields = true, .allocate = .alloc_always },\n                ) catch continue; // Skip malformed entries\n\n                // If no ID, generate one\n                var issue = parsed.value;\n                if (issue.id.len == 0) {\n                    const new_id = try generator.generate(allocator, issue_count);\n                    allocator.free(issue.id);\n                    issue.id = new_id;\n                    issue_count += 1;\n                }\n\n                try issues_to_add.append(allocator, issue);\n            }\n        },\n    }\n\n    if (issues_to_add.items.len == 0) {\n        if (structured_output) {\n            try output.printJson(BatchResult{\n                .success = true,\n                .issues_created = 0,\n                .message = \"no issues to add\",\n            });\n        } else if (!global.quiet) {\n            try output.info(\"No issues to add\", .{});\n        }\n        return;\n    }\n\n    // Insert all issues (single save at end)\n    var created_ids: std.ArrayListUnmanaged([]const u8) = .{};\n    defer {\n        for (created_ids.items) |id| {\n            allocator.free(id);\n        }\n        created_ids.deinit(allocator);\n    }\n\n    for (issues_to_add.items) |issue| {\n        store.insert(issue) catch |err| switch (err) {\n              return BatchError.StorageError;\n            },\n        };\n        const id_copy = try allocator.dupe(u8, issue.id);\n        try created_ids.append(allocator, id_copy);\n    }\n\n    // Single atomic save\n    if (!global.no_auto_flush) {\n        store.saveToFile() catch {\n            try common.outputErrorTyped(BatchResult, &output, structured_output, \"failed to save issues\");\n            return BatchError.StorageError;\n        };\n    }\n\n    // Output result\n    if (structured_output) {\n        try output.printJson(BatchResult{\n            .success = true,\n            .issues_created = created_ids.items.len,\n            .ids = created_ids.items,\n        });\n    } else if (global.quiet) {\n        for (created_ids.items) |id| {\n            try output.raw(id);\n            try output.raw(\"\\n\");\n        }\n    } else {\n        try output.success(\"Created {d} issue(s)\", .{created_ids.items.len});\n    }\n}\n\n/// Run the import command.\n/// Imports issues from a JSONL file with single lock acquisition.\npub fn runImport(\n    import_args: args.ImportArgs,\n    global: args.GlobalOptions,\n    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,\n) !void {\n    var output = common.initOutput(allocator, global);\n    const structured_output = global.isStructuredOutput();\n\n    // Determine workspace path\n    const beads_dir = global.data_path orelse \".beads\";\n    const issues_path = try std.fs.path.join(allocator, &.{ beads_dir, \"issues.jsonl\" });\n    defer allocator.free(issues_path);\n\n    // Check if workspace is initialized\n    std.fs.cwd().access(issues_path, .{}) catch |err| {\n        if (err == error.FileNotFound) {\n            try common.outputErrorTyped(ImportResult, &output, Run 'bz init' first.\");\n            return BatchError.WorkspaceNotInitialized;\n        }\n        try common.outputErrorTyped(ImportResult, &output, structured_output, \"cannot access workspace\");\n        return BatchError.StorageError;\n    };\n\n    // Check for merge conflict markers in import file\n    if (try hasMergeConflicts(import_args.file, allocator)) {\n        try common.outputErrorTyped(ImportResult, &output, structured_output, \"import file contains merge conflict markers\");\n        return BatchError.InvalidInput;\n    }\n\n    // Read and parse the import file\n    var import_jsonl = JsonlFile.init(import_args.file, allocator);\n    const imported_issues = import_jsonl.readAllWithRecovery() catch {\n        try common.outputErrorTyped(ImportResult, &output, structured_output, \"failed to read import file\");\n        return BatchError.FileReadError;\n    };\n    defer {\n        for (imported_issues.issues) |*issue| {\n            var i = issue.*;\n            i.deinit(allocator);\n        }\n        allocator.free(imported_issues.issues);\n        if (imported_issues.corrupt_lines.len > 0) {\n            allocator.free(imported_issues.corrupt_lines);\n        }\n    }\n\n    if (import_args.dry_run) {\n        // Dry run - just report what would be imported\n        if (structured_output) {\n            try output.printJson(ImportResult{\n                .success = true,\n                .issues_imported = imported_issues.issues.len,\n                .issues_skipped = imported_issues.corruption_count,\n                .message = \"dry run - no changes made\",\n            });\n        } else if (!global.quiet) {\n            try output.info(\"Would import {d} Load existing issues\n    var store = IssueStore.init(allocator, issues_path);\n    defer store.deinit();\n\n    store.loadFromFile() catch |err| {\n        if (err != error.FileNotFound) {\n            try common.outputErrorTyped(ImportResult, &output, structured_output, \"failed to load existing issues\");\n            return BatchError.StorageError;\n        }\n    };\n\n    var imported_count: usize = 0;\n    var skipped_count: usize = 0;\n    var updated_count: usize = 0;\n\n    const now = std.time.timestamp();\n\n    for (imported_issues.issues) |issue| {\n        if (import_args.merge) {\n            // Merge mode: update if exists, insert if not\n            if (try store.exists(issue.id)) {\n                // Update existing issue\n                store.update(issue.id, .{\n                    .title = issue.title,\n                    .description = issue.description,\n                    .status = issue.status,\n                    .priority = issue.priority,\n                    .issue_type = issue.issue_type,\n                    .assignee = issue.assignee,\n                }, now) catch {\n                    skipped_count += 1;\n                    continue;\n                };\n                updated_count += 1;\n            } else {\n                store.insert(issue) catch {\n                    skipped_count += 1;\n                    continue;\n                };\n                imported_count += 1;\n            }\n        } else {\n            // Replace mode: skip if exists\n            if (try store.exists(issue.id)) {\n                skipped_count += 1;\n                continue;\n            }\n            store.insert(issue) catch {\n                skipped_count += 1;\n                continue;\n            };\n            imported_count += 1;\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Single atomic save\n    if (!global.no_auto_flush) {\n        store.saveToFile() catch {\n            try common.outputErrorTyped(ImportResult, &output, structured_output, \"failed to save issues\");\n            return BatchError.StorageError;\n        };\n    }\n\n    // Output result\n    if (structured_output) {\n        try output.printJson(ImportResult{\n            .success = true,\n            .issues_imported = imported_count,\n            .issues_updated = if (import_args.merge) updated_count else null,\n            .issues_skipped = skipped_count + imported_issues.corruption_count,\n        });\n    } else if (!global.quiet) {\n        if (import_args.merge and updated_count > 0) {\n            try output.success(\"Imported {d}, updated {d}, skipped {d} issue(s)\", .{\n                imported_count,\n                updated_count,\n                skipped_count,\n            });\n        } else {\n            try output.success(\"Imported {d}, skipped {d} issue(s)\", .{ imported_count, skipped_count });\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/// Read file content into a buffer.\nfn readFileContent(path: []const u8, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) ![]u8 {\n    const file = try std.fs.cwd().openFile(path, .{});\n    defer file.close();\n    return try file.readToEndAlloc(allocator, 100 * 1024 * 1024); // 100MB max\n}\n\n\n/// Check if a file contains git merge conflict markers.\nfn hasMergeConflicts(path: []const u8, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) !bool {\n    const file = std.fs.cwd().openFile(path, .{}) catch |err| switch (err) {\n        error.FileNotFound => return false,\n        else => return err,\n    };\n    defer file.close();\n\n    const content = try file.readToEndAlloc(allocator, 1024 * 1024 * 10);\n    defer allocator.free(content);\n\n    if (std.mem.indexOf(u8, content, \"<<<<<<<\") != null) return true;\n    if (std.mem.indexOf(u8, content, \"=======\") != null) return true;\n    if (std.mem.indexOf(u8, content, \">>>>>>>\") != null) return true;\n\n    return false;\n}\n\n/// Get the default actor name from environment.\nfn getDefaultActor() ?[]const u8 {\n    const builtin = @import(\"builtin\");\n    if (builtin.os.tag == .windows) return null;\n    return std.posix.getenv(\"USER\") orelse std.posix.getenv(\"USERNAME\");\n}\n\n/// Read the ID prefix from config.yaml, defaulting to \"bd\".\nfn getConfigPrefix(allocator: std.mem.Allocator, beads_dir: []const u8) ![]u8 {\n    const config_path = try std.fs.path.join(allocator, &.{ beads_dir, \"config.yaml\" });\n    defer allocator.free(config_path);\n\n    const file = std.fs.cwd().openFile(config_path, .{}) catch {\n        return try allocator.dupe(u8, \"bd\");\n    };\n    defer file.close();\n\n    const content = file.readToEndAlloc(allocator, 4096) catch {\n        return try allocator.dupe(u8, \"bd\");\n    };\n    defer allocator.free(content);\n\n    if (std.mem.indexOf(u8, content, \"prefix:\")) |prefix_pos| {\n        const after_prefix = content[prefix_pos + 7 ..];\n        var i: usize = 0;\n        while (i < after_prefix.len and (after_prefix[i] == ' ' or after_prefix[i] == '\\t')) {\n            i += 1;\n        }\n\n        if (i < after_prefix.len) {\n            if (after_prefix[i] == '\"') {\n                i += 1;\n                const start = i;\n                while (i < after_prefix.len and after_prefix[i] != '\"' and after_prefix[i] != '\\n') {\n                    i += 1;\n                }\n                if (i > start) {\n                    return try allocator.dupe(u8, after_prefix[start..i]);\n                }\n            } else {\n                const start = i;\n                while (i < after_prefix.len and after_prefix[i] != '\\n' and after_prefix[i] != ' ' and after_prefix[i] != '\\t') {\n                    i += 1;\n                }\n                if (i > start) {\n                    return try allocator.dupe(u8, after_prefix[start..i]);\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    return try allocator.dupe(u8, \"bd\");\n}\n\n// --- Tests ---\n\ntest Batch operations for beads_zig.\n//!\n//! - `bz add-batch` - Create multiple issues from stdin/file with single lock\n//! - `bz import <file>` - Import issues from JSONL file with single lock\n//!\n//! These operations reduce lock contention for bulk operations by acquiring\n//! a single lock, performing all insertions, and releasing.\n\nconst std = @import(\"std\");\nconst models = @import(\"../models/mod.zig\");\nconst storage = @import(\"../storage/mod.zig\");\nconst id_gen = @import(\"../id/mod.zig\");\nconst common = @import(\"common.zig\");\nconst args = @import(\"args.zig\");\nconst test_util = @import(\"../test_util.zig\");\n\nconst Issue = models.Issue;\nconst Priority = models.Priority;\nconst IssueType = models.IssueType;\nconst IssueStore = storage.IssueStore;\nconst JsonlFile = storage.JsonlFile;\nconst IdGenerator = id_gen.IdGenerator;\n\npub const BatchError = error{\n    WorkspaceNotInitialized,\n    StorageError,\n    InvalidInput,\n    FileReadError,\n    NoIssuesToAdd,\n    OutOfMemory,\n};\n\npub const BatchResult = struct {\n    success: bool,\n    issues_created: ?usize = null,\n    issues_imported: ?usize = null,\n    issues_skipped: ?usize = null,\n    ids: ?[]const []const u8 = null,\n    message: ?[]const u8 = null,\n};\n\npub const ImportResult = struct {\n    success: bool,\n    issues_imported: ?usize = null,\n    issues_skipped: ?usize = null,\n    issues_updated: ?usize = null,\n    message: ?[]const u8 = null,\n};\n\n/// Run the add-batch command.\n/// Creates multiple issues with a single lock acquisition and fsync.\npub fn runAddBatch(\n    batch_args: args.AddBatchArgs,\n    global: args.GlobalOptions,\n    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,\n) !void {\n    var output = common.initOutput(allocator, global);\n    const structured_output = global.isStructuredOutput();\n\n    // Determine workspace path\n    const beads_dir = global.data_path orelse \".beads\";\n    const issues_path = try std.fs.path.join(allocator, &.{ beads_dir, \"issues.jsonl\" });\n    defer allocator.free(issues_path);\n\n    // Check if workspace is initialized\n    std.fs.cwd().access(issues_path, .{}) catch |err| {\n        if (err == error.FileNotFound) {\n            try common.outputErrorTyped(BatchResult, &output, structured_output, \"workspace not initialized. Run 'bz init' first.\");\n            return BatchError.WorkspaceNotInitialized;\n        }\n        try common.outputErrorTyped(BatchResult, &output, structured_output, \"cannot access workspace\");\n        return BatchError.StorageError;\n    };\n\n    // Read input from file\n    const file_path = batch_args.file orelse {\n        try common.outputErrorTyped(BatchResult, &output, structured_output, \"file path required. Use 'bz add-batch <file>' or 'bz add-batch --file <file>'\");\n        return BatchError.InvalidInput;\n    };\n\n    const input_content = readFileContent(file_path, allocator) catch {\n        try common.outputErrorTyped(BatchResult, &output, structured_output, \"failed to read input file\");\n        return BatchError.FileReadError;\n    };\n    defer allocator.free(input_content);\n\n    // Parse input based on format\n    var issues_to_add: std.ArrayListUnmanaged(Issue) = .{};\n    defer {\n        for (issues_to_add.items) |*issue| {\n            issue.deinit(allocator);\n        }\n        issues_to_add.deinit(allocator);\n    }\n\n    // Load existing issues to get count for ID generation\n    var store = IssueStore.init(allocator, issues_path);\n    defer store.deinit();\n\n    store.loadFromFile() catch |err| {\n        if (err != error.FileNotFound) {\n            try common.outputErrorTyped(BatchResult, &output, structured_output, \"failed to load issues\");\n            return BatchError.StorageError;\n        }\n    };\n\n    // Get config prefix\n    const prefix = try getConfigPrefix(allocator, beads_dir);\n    defer allocator.free(prefix);\n\n    // Get actor\n    const actor = global.actor orelse getDefaultActor();\n\n    const now = std.time.timestamp();\n    var generator = IdGenerator.init(prefix);\n    var issue_count = store.countTotal();\n\n    // Parse input and create issues\n    switch (batch_args.format) {\n        .titles => {\n            var line_iter = std.mem.splitScalar(u8, input_content, '\\n');\n            while (line_iter.next()) |line| {\n                const trimmed = std.mem.trim(u8, line, \" \\t\\r\");\n                if (trimmed.len == 0) continue;\n                if (trimmed.len > 500) continue; // Skip titles that are too long\n\n                const issue_id = try generator.generate(allocator, issue_count);\n                errdefer allocator.free(issue_id);\n                issue_count += 1;\n\n                var issue = Issue.init(issue_id, trimmed, now);\n                issue.created_by = actor;\n\n                // Clone strings for owned storage\n                const cloned = try issue.clone(allocator);\n                allocator.free(issue_id); // clone made its own copy\n                try issues_to_add.append(allocator, cloned);\n            }\n        },\n        .jsonl => {\n            var line_iter = std.mem.splitScalar(u8, input_content, '\\n');\n            while (line_iter.next()) |line| {\n                const trimmed = std.mem.trim(u8, line, \" \\t\\r\");\n                if (trimmed.len == 0) continue;\n\n                // Parse as Issue JSON\n                const parsed = std.json.parseFromSlice(\n                    Issue,\n                    allocator,\n                    trimmed,\n                    .{ .ignore_unknown_fields = true, .allocate = .alloc_always },\n                ) catch continue; // Skip malformed entries\n\n                // If no ID, generate one\n                var issue = parsed.value;\n                if (issue.id.len == 0) {\n                    const new_id = try generator.generate(allocator, issue_count);\n                    allocator.free(issue.id);\n                    issue.id = new_id;\n                    issue_count += 1;\n                }\n\n                try issues_to_add.append(allocator, issue);\n            }\n        },\n    }\n\n    if (issues_to_add.items.len == 0) {\n        if (structured_output) {\n            try output.printJson(BatchResult{\n                .success = true,\n                .issues_created = 0,\n                .message = \"no issues to add\",\n            });\n        } else if (!global.quiet) {\n            try output.info(\"No issues to add\", .{});\n        }\n        return;\n    }\n\n    // Insert all issues (single save at end)\n    var created_ids: std.ArrayListUnmanaged([]const u8) = .{};\n    defer {\n        for (created_ids.items) |id| {\n            allocator.free(id);\n        }\n        created_ids.deinit(allocator);\n    }\n\n    for (issues_to_add.items) |issue| {\n        store.insert(issue) catch |err| switch (err) {\n            error.DuplicateId => continue, // Skip duplicates\n            else => {\n                try common.outputErrorTyped(BatchResult, &output, structured_output, \"failed to insert issue\");\n                return BatchError.StorageError;\n            },\n        };\n        const id_copy = try allocator.dupe(u8, issue.id);\n        try created_ids.append(allocator, id_copy);\n    }\n\n    // Single atomic save\n    if (!global.no_auto_flush) {\n        store.saveToFile() catch {\n            try common.outputErrorTyped(BatchResult, &output, structured_output, \"failed to save issues\");\n            return BatchError.StorageError;\n        };\n    }\n\n    // Output result\n    if (structured_output) {\n        try output.printJson(BatchResult{\n            .success = true,\n            .issues_created = created_ids.items.len,\n            .ids = created_ids.items,\n        });\n    } else if (global.quiet) {\n        for (created_ids.items) |id| {\n            try output.raw(id);\n            try output.raw(\"\\n\");\n        }\n    } else {\n        try output.success(\"Created {d} issue(s)\", .{created_ids.items.len});\n    }\n}\n\n/// Run the import command.\n/// Imports issues from a JSONL file with single lock acquisition.\npub fn runImport(\n    import_args: args.ImportArgs,\n    global: args.GlobalOptions,\n    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,\n) !void {\n    var output = common.initOutput(allocator, global);\n    const structured_output = global.isStructuredOutput();\n\n    // Determine workspace path\n    const beads_dir = global.data_path orelse \".beads\";\n    const issues_path = try std.fs.path.join(allocator, &.{ beads_dir, \"issues.jsonl\" });\n    defer allocator.free(issues_path);\n\n    // Check if workspace is initialized\n    std.fs.cwd().access(issues_path, .{}) catch |err| {\n        if (err == error.FileNotFound) {\n            try common.outputErrorTyped(ImportResult, &output, structured_output, \"workspace not initialized. Run 'bz init' first.\");\n            return BatchError.WorkspaceNotInitialized;\n        }\n        try common.outputErrorTyped(ImportResult, &output, structured_output, \"cannot access workspace\");\n        return BatchError.StorageError;\n    };\n\n    // Check for merge conflict markers in import file\n    if (try hasMergeConflicts(import_args.file, allocator)) {\n        try common.outputErrorTyped(ImportResult, &output, structured_output, \"import file contains merge conflict markers\");\n        return BatchError.InvalidInput;\n    }\n\n    // Read and parse the import file\n    var import_jsonl = JsonlFile.init(import_args.file, allocator);\n    const imported_issues = import_jsonl.readAllWithRecovery() catch {\n        try common.outputErrorTyped(ImportResult, &output, structured_output, \"failed to read import file\");\n        return BatchError.FileReadError;\n    };\n    defer {\n        for (imported_issues.issues) |*issue| {\n            var i = issue.*;\n            i.deinit(allocator);\n        }\n        allocator.free(imported_issues.issues);\n        if (imported_issues.corrupt_lines.len > 0) {\n            allocator.free(imported_issues.corrupt_lines);\n        }\n    }\n\n    if (import_args.dry_run) {\n        // Dry run - just report what would be imported\n        if (structured_output) {\n            try output.printJson(ImportResult{\n                .success = true,\n                .issues_imported = imported_issues.issues.len,\n                .issues_skipped = imported_issues.corruption_count,\n                .message = \"dry run - no changes made\",\n            });\n        } else if (!global.quiet) {\n            try output.info(\"Would import {d} issue(s), skip {d} corrupt entries\", .{\n                imported_issues.issues.len,\n                imported_issues.corruption_count,\n            });\n        }\n        return;\n    }\n\n    // Load existing issues\n    var store = IssueStore.init(allocator, issues_path);\n    defer store.deinit();\n\n    store.loadFromFile() catch |err| {\n        if (err != error.FileNotFound) {\n            try common.outputErrorTyped(ImportResult, &output, structured_output, \"failed to load existing issues\");\n            return BatchError.StorageError;\n        }\n    };\n\n    var imported_count: usize = 0;\n    var skipped_count: usize = 0;\n    var updated_count: usize = 0;\n\n    const now = std.time.timestamp();\n\n    for (imported_issues.issues) |issue| {\n        if (import_args.merge) {\n            // Merge mode: update if exists, insert if not\n            if (try store.exists(issue.id)) {\n                // Update existing issue\n                store.update(issue.id, .{\n                    .title = issue.title,\n                    .description = issue.description,\n                    .status = issue.status,\n                    .priority = issue.priority,\n                    .issue_type = issue.issue_type,\n                    .assignee = issue.assignee,\n                }, now) catch {\n                    skipped_count += 1;\n                    continue;\n                };\n                updated_count += 1;\n            } else {\n                store.insert(issue) catch {\n                    skipped_count += 1;\n                    continue;\n                };\n                imported_count += 1;\n            }\n        } else {\n            // Replace mode: skip if exists\n            if (try store.exists(issue.id)) {\n                skipped_count += 1;\n                continue;\n            }\n            store.insert(issue) catch {\n                skipped_count += 1;\n                continue;\n            };\n            imported_count += 1;\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Single atomic save\n    if (!global.no_auto_flush) {\n        store.saveToFile() catch {\n            try common.outputErrorTyped(ImportResult, &output, structured_output, \"failed to save issues\");\n            return BatchError.StorageError;\n        };\n    }\n\n    // Output result\n    if (structured_output) {\n        try output.printJson(ImportResult{\n            .success = true,\n            .issues_imported = imported_count,\n            .issues_updated = if (import_args.merge) updated_count else null,\n            .issues_skipped = skipped_count + imported_issues.corruption_count,\n        });\n    } else if (!global.quiet) {\n        if (import_args.merge and updated_count > 0) {\n            try output.success(\"Imported {d}, updated {d}, skipped {d} issue(s)\", .{\n                imported_count,\n                updated_count,\n                skipped_count,\n            });\n        } else {\n            try output.success(\"Imported {d}, skipped {d} issue(s)\", .{ imported_count, skipped_count });\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/// Read file content into a buffer.\nfn readFileContent(path: []const u8, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) ![]u8 {\n    const file = try std.fs.cwd().openFile(path, .{});\n    defer file.close();\n    return try file.readToEndAlloc(allocator, 100 * 1024 * 1024); // 100MB max\n}\n\n/// Check if a file contains git merge conflict markers.\nfn hasMergeConflicts(path: []const u8, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) !bool {\n    const file = std.fs.cwd().openFile(path, .{}) catch |err| switch (err) {\n        error.FileNotFound => return false,\n        else => return err,\n    };\n    defer file.close();\n\n    const content = try file.readToEndAlloc(allocator, 1024 * 1024 * 10);\n    defer allocator.free(content);\n\n    if (std.mem.indexOf(u8, content, \"<<<<<<<\") != null) return true;\n    if (std.mem.indexOf(u8, content, \"=======\") != null) return true;\n    if (std.mem.indexOf(u8, content, \">>>>>>>\") != null) return true;\n\n    return false;\n}\n\n/// Get the default actor name from environment.\nfn getDefaultActor() ?[]const u8 {\n    const builtin = @import(\"builtin\");\n    if (builtin.os.tag == .windows) return null;\n    return std.posix.getenv(\"USER\") orelse std.posix.getenv(\"USERNAME\");\n}\n\n/// Read the ID prefix from config.yaml, defaulting to \"bd\".\nfn getConfigPrefix(allocator: std.mem.Allocator, beads_dir: []const u8) ![]u8 {\n    const config_path = try std.fs.path.join(allocator, &.{ beads_dir, \"config.yaml\" });\n    defer allocator.free(config_path);\n\n    const file = std.fs.cwd().openFile(config_path, .{}) catch {\n        return try allocator.dupe(u8, \"bd\");\n    };\n    defer file.close();\n\n    const content = file.readToEndAlloc(allocator, 4096) catch {\n        return try allocator.dupe(u8, \"bd\");\n    };\n    defer allocator.free(content);\n\n    if (std.mem.indexOf(u8, content, \"prefix:\")) |prefix_pos| {\n        const after_prefix = content[prefix_pos + 7 ..];\n        var i: usize = 0;\n        while (i < after_prefix.len and (after_prefix[i] == ' ' or after_prefix[i] == '\\t')) {\n            i += 1;\n        }\n\n        if (i < after_prefix.len) {\n            if (after_prefix[i] == '\"') {\n                i += 1;\n                const start = i;\n                while (i < after_prefix.len and after_prefix[i] != '\"' and after_prefix[i] != '\\n') {\n                    i += 1;\n                }\n                if (i > start) {\n                    return try allocator.dupe(u8, after_prefix[start..i]);\n                }\n            } else {\n                const start = i;\n                while (i < after_prefix.len and after_prefix[i] != '\\n' and after_prefix[i] != ' ' and after_prefix[i] != '\\t') {\n                    i += 1;\n                }\n                if (i > start) {\n                    return try allocator.dupe(u8, after_prefix[start..i]);\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    return try allocator.dupe(u8, \"bd\");\n}\n\n// --- Tests ---\n\ntest \"BatchError enum exists\" {\n    const err: BatchError = BatchError.WorkspaceNotInitialized;\n    try std.testing.expect(err == BatchError.WorkspaceNotInitialized);\n}\n\ntest \"BatchResult struct works\" {\n    const result = BatchResult{\n        .success = true,\n        .issues_created = 5,\n    };\n    try std.testing.expect(result.success);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 5), result.issues_created.?);\n}\n\ntest \"ImportResult struct works\" {\n    const result = ImportResult{\n        .success = true,\n        .issues_imported = 10,\n        .issues_skipped = 2,\n    };\n    try std.testing.expect(result.success);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 10), result.issues_imported.?);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 2), result.issues_skipped.?);\n}\n\ntest \"runAddBatch detects uninitialized workspace\" {\n    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n\n    const batch_args = args.AddBatchArgs{};\n    const global = args.GlobalOptions{ .silent = true, .data_path = \"/nonexistent/path\" };\n\n    const result = runAddBatch(batch_args, global, allocator);\n    try std.testing.expectError(BatchError.WorkspaceNotInitialized, result);\n}\n\ntest \"runImport detects uninitialized workspace\" {\n    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n\n    const import_args = args.ImportArgs{ .file = \"test.jsonl\" };\n    const global = args.GlobalOptions{ .silent = true, .data_path = \"/nonexistent/path\" };\n\n    const result = runImport(import_args, global, allocator);\n    try std.testing.expectError(BatchError.WorkspaceNotInitialized, result);\n}\n\ntest \"hasMergeConflicts returns false for missing file\" {\n    const has_conflicts = try hasMergeConflicts(\"/nonexistent/path.jsonl\", std.testing.allocator);\n    try std.testing.expect(!has_conflicts);\n}\n\ntest \"hasMergeConflicts returns false for clean file\" {\n    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n    const test_dir = try test_util.createTestDir(allocator, \"batch_clean\");\n    defer allocator.free(test_dir);\n    defer test_util.cleanupTestDir(test_dir);\n\n    const test_path = try std.fs.path.join(allocator, &.{ test_dir, \"clean.jsonl\" });\n    defer allocator.free(test_path);\n\n    const file = try std.fs.cwd().createFile(test_path, .{});\n    try file.writeAll(\"{\\\"id\\\":\\\"bd-test\\\",\\\"title\\\":\\\"Test\\\"}\\n\");\n    file.close();\n\n    const has_conflicts = try hasMergeConflicts(test_path, allocator);\n    try std.testing.expect(!has_conflicts);\n}\n\ntest \"hasMergeConflicts returns true for conflicted file\" {\n    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n    const test_dir = try test_util.createTestDir(allocator, \"batch_conflict\");\n    defer allocator.free(test_dir);\n    defer test_util.cleanupTestDir(test_dir);\n\n    const test_path = try std.fs.path.join(allocator, &.{ HEAD\\n{\\\"id\\\":\\\"bd-test1\\\"}\\n=======\\n{\\\"id\\\":\\\"bd-test2\\\"}\\n>>>>>>> branch\\n\");\n    file.close();\n\n    const has_conflicts = try hasMergeConflicts(test_path, allocator);\n    try std.testing.expect(has_conflicts);\n}\n\ntest \"runAddBatch creates issues from titles format\" {\n    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n    const test_dir = try test_util.createTestDir(allocator, \"batch_titles\");\n    defer allocator.free(test_dir);\n    defer test_util.cleanupTestDir(test_dir);\n\n    // Create workspace\n    const data_path = try Batch operations for beads_zig.\n//!\n//! - `bz add-batch` - Create multiple issues from stdin/file with single lock\n//! - `bz import <file>` - Import issues from JSONL file with single lock\n//!\n//! These operations reduce lock contention for bulk operations by acquiring\n//! a single lock, performing all insertions, and releasing.\n\nconst std = @import(\"std\");\nconst models = @import(\"../models/mod.zig\");\nconst storage = @import(\"../storage/mod.zig\");\nconst id_gen = @import(\"../id/mod.zig\");\nconst common = @import(\"common.zig\");\nconst args = @import(\"args.zig\");\nconst test_util = @import(\"../test_util.zig\");\n\nconst Issue = models.Issue;\nconst Priority = models.Priority;\nconst IssueType = models.IssueType;\nconst IssueStore = storage.IssueStore;\nconst JsonlFile = storage.JsonlFile;\nconst IdGenerator = id_gen.IdGenerator;\n\npub const BatchError = error{\n    WorkspaceNotInitialized,\n    StorageError,\n    InvalidInput,\n    FileReadError,\n    NoIssuesToAdd,\n    OutOfMemory,\n};\n\npub const BatchResult = struct {\n    success: bool,\n    issues_created: ?usize = null,\n    issues_imported: ?usize = null,\n    issues_skipped: ?usize = null,\n    ids: ?[]const []const u8 = null,\n    message: ?[]const u8 = null,\n};\n\npub const ImportResult = struct {\n    success: bool,\n    issues_imported: ?usize = null,\n    issues_skipped: ?usize = null,\n    issues_updated: ?usize = null,\n    message: ?[]const u8 = null,\n};\n\n/// Run the add-batch command.\n/// Creates multiple issues with a single lock acquisition and fsync.\npub fn runAddBatch(\n    batch_args: args.AddBatchArgs,\n    global: args.GlobalOptions,\n    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,\n) !void {\n    var output = common.initOutput(allocator, global);\n    const structured_output = global.isStructuredOutput();\n\n    // Determine workspace path\n    const beads_dir = global.data_path orelse \".beads\";\n    const issues_path = try std.fs.path.join(allocator, &.{ beads_dir, \"issues.jsonl\" });\n    defer allocator.free(issues_path);\n\n    // Check if workspace is initialized\n    std.fs.cwd().access(issues_path, .{}) catch |err| {\n        if (err == error.FileNotFound) {\n            try common.outputErrorTyped(BatchResult, &output, structured_output, \"workspace not initialized. Run 'bz init' first.\");\n            return BatchError.WorkspaceNotInitialized;\n        }\n        try common.outputErrorTyped(BatchResult, &output, structured_output, \"cannot access workspace\");\n        return BatchError.StorageError;\n    };\n\n    // Read input from file\n    const file_path = batch_args.file orelse {\n        try common.outputErrorTyped(BatchResult, &output, structured_output, \"file path required. Use 'bz add-batch <file>' or 'bz add-batch --file <file>'\");\n        return BatchError.InvalidInput;\n    };\n\n    const input_content = readFileContent(file_path, allocator) catch {\n        try common.outputErrorTyped(BatchResult, &output, structured_output, \"failed to read input file\");\n        return BatchError.FileReadError;\n    };\n    defer allocator.free(input_content);\n\n    // Parse input based on format\n    var issues_to_add: std.ArrayListUnmanaged(Issue) = .{};\n    defer {\n        for (issues_to_add.items) |*issue| {\n            issue.deinit(allocator);\n        }\n        issues_to_add.deinit(allocator);\n    }\n\n    // Load existing issues to get count for ID generation\n    var store = IssueStore.init(allocator, issues_path);\n    defer store.deinit();\n\n    store.loadFromFile() catch |err| {\n        if (err != error.FileNotFound) {\n            try common.outputErrorTyped(BatchResult, &output, structured_output, \"failed to load issues\");\n            return BatchError.StorageError;\n        }\n    };\n\n    // Get config prefix\n    const prefix = try getConfigPrefix(allocator, beads_dir);\n    defer allocator.free(prefix);\n\n    // Get actor\n    const actor = global.actor orelse getDefaultActor();\n\n    const now = std.time.timestamp();\n    var generator = IdGenerator.init(prefix);\n    var issue_count = store.countTotal();\n\n    // Parse input and create issues\n    switch (batch_args.format) {\n        .titles => {\n            var line_iter = std.mem.splitScalar(u8, input_content, '\\n');\n            while (line_iter.next()) |line| {\n                const trimmed = std.mem.trim(u8, line, \" \\t\\r\");\n                if (trimmed.len == 0) continue;\n                if (trimmed.len > 500) continue; // Skip titles that are too long\n\n                const issue_id = try generator.generate(allocator, issue_count);\n                errdefer allocator.free(issue_id);\n                issue_count += 1;\n\n                var issue = Issue.init(issue_id, trimmed, now);\n                issue.created_by = actor;\n\n                // Clone strings for owned storage\n                const cloned = try issue.clone(allocator);\n                allocator.free(issue_id); // clone made its own copy\n                try issues_to_add.append(allocator, cloned);\n            }\n        },\n        .jsonl => {\n            var line_iter = std.mem.splitScalar(u8, input_content, '\\n');\n            while (line_iter.next()) |line| {\n                const trimmed = std.mem.trim(u8, line, \" \\t\\r\");\n                if (trimmed.len == 0) continue;\n\n                // Parse as Issue JSON\n                const parsed = std.json.parseFromSlice(\n                    Issue,\n                    allocator,\n                    trimmed,\n                    .{ .ignore_unknown_fields = true, .allocate = .alloc_always },\n                ) catch continue; // Skip malformed entries\n\n                // If no ID, generate one\n                var issue = parsed.value;\n                if (issue.id.len == 0) {\n                    const new_id = try generator.generate(allocator, issue_count);\n                    allocator.free(issue.id);\n                    issue.id = new_id;\n                    issue_count += 1;\n                }\n\n                try issues_to_add.append(allocator, issue);\n            }\n        },\n    }\n\n    if (issues_to_add.items.len == 0) {\n        if (structured_output) {\n            try output.printJson(BatchResult{\n                .success = true,\n                .issues_created = 0,\n                .message = \"no issues to add\",\n            });\n        } else if (!global.quiet) {\n            try output.info(\"No issues to add\", .{});\n        }\n        return;\n    }\n\n    // Insert all issues (single save at end)\n    var created_ids: std.ArrayListUnmanaged([]const u8) = .{};\n    defer {\n        for (created_ids.items) |id| {\n            allocator.free(id);\n        }\n        created_ids.deinit(allocator);\n    }\n\n    for (issues_to_add.items) |issue| {\n        store.insert(issue) catch |err| switch (err) {\n            error.DuplicateId => continue, // Skip duplicates\n            else => {\n                try common.outputErrorTyped(BatchResult, &output, structured_output, \"failed to insert issue\");\n                return BatchError.StorageError;\n            },\n        };\n        const id_copy = try allocator.dupe(u8, issue.id);\n        try created_ids.append(allocator, id_copy);\n    }\n\n    // Single atomic save\n    if (!global.no_auto_flush) {\n        store.saveToFile() catch {\n            try common.outputErrorTyped(BatchResult, &output, structured_output, \"failed to save issues\");\n            return BatchError.StorageError;\n        };\n    }\n\n    // Output result\n    if (structured_output) {\n        try output.printJson(BatchResult{\n            .success = true,\n            .issues_created = created_ids.items.len,\n            .ids = created_ids.items,\n        });\n    } else if (global.quiet) {\n        for (created_ids.items) |id| {\n            try output.raw(id);\n            try output.raw(\"\\n\");\n        }\n    } else {\n        try output.success(\"Created {d} issue(s)\", .{created_ids.items.len});\n    }\n}\n\n/// Run the import command.\n/// Imports issues from a JSONL file with single lock acquisition.\npub fn runImport(\n    import_args: args.ImportArgs,\n    global: args.GlobalOptions,\n    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,\n) !void {\n    var output = common.initOutput(allocator, global);\n    const structured_output = global.isStructuredOutput();\n\n    // Determine workspace path\n    const beads_dir = global.data_path orelse \".beads\";\n    const issues_path = try std.fs.path.join(allocator, &.{ beads_dir, \"issues.jsonl\" });\n    defer allocator.free(issues_path);\n\n    // Check if workspace is initialized\n    std.fs.cwd().access(issues_path, .{}) catch |err| {\n        if (err == error.FileNotFound) {\n            try common.outputErrorTyped(ImportResult, &output, structured_output, \"workspace not initialized. Run 'bz init' first.\");\n            return BatchError.WorkspaceNotInitialized;\n        }\n        try common.outputErrorTyped(ImportResult, &output, structured_output, \"cannot access workspace\");\n        return BatchError.StorageError;\n    };\n\n    // Check for merge conflict markers in import file\n    if (try hasMergeConflicts(import_args.file, allocator)) {\n        try common.outputErrorTyped(ImportResult, &output, structured_output, \"import file contains merge conflict markers\");\n        return BatchError.InvalidInput;\n    }\n\n    // Read and parse the import file\n    var import_jsonl = JsonlFile.init(import_args.file, allocator);\n    const imported_issues = import_jsonl.readAllWithRecovery() catch {\n        try common.outputErrorTyped(ImportResult, &output, structured_output, \"failed to read import file\");\n        return BatchError.FileReadError;\n    };\n    defer {\n        for (imported_issues.issues) |*issue| {\n            var i = issue.*;\n            i.deinit(allocator);\n        }\n        allocator.free(imported_issues.issues);\n        if (imported_issues.corrupt_lines.len > 0) {\n            allocator.free(imported_issues.corrupt_lines);\n        }\n    }\n\n    if (import_args.dry_run) {\n        // Dry run - just report what would be imported\n        if (structured_output) {\n            try output.printJson(ImportResult{\n                .success = true,\n                .issues_imported = imported_issues.issues.len,\n                .issues_skipped = imported_issues.corruption_count,\n                .message = \"dry run - no changes made\",\n            });\n        } else if (!global.quiet) {\n            try output.info(\"Would import {d} issue(s), skip {d} corrupt entries\", .{\n                imported_issues.issues.len,\n                imported_issues.corruption_count,\n            });\n        }\n        return;\n    }\n\n    // Load existing issues\n    var store = IssueStore.init(allocator, issues_path);\n    defer store.deinit();\n\n    store.loadFromFile() catch |err| {\n        if (err != error.FileNotFound) {\n            try common.outputErrorTyped(ImportResult, &output, structured_output, \"failed to load existing issues\");\n            return BatchError.StorageError;\n        }\n    };\n\n    var imported_count: usize = 0;\n    var skipped_count: usize = 0;\n    var updated_count: usize = 0;\n\n    const now = std.time.timestamp();\n\n    for (imported_issues.issues) |issue| {\n        if (import_args.merge) {\n            // Merge mode: update if exists, insert if not\n            if (try store.exists(issue.id)) {\n                // Update existing issue\n                store.update(issue.id, .{\n                    .title = issue.title,\n                    .description = issue.description,\n                    .status = issue.status,\n                    .priority = issue.priority,\n                    .issue_type = issue.issue_type,\n                    .assignee = issue.assignee,\n                }, now) catch {\n                    skipped_count += 1;\n                    continue;\n                };\n                updated_count += 1;\n            } else {\n                store.insert(issue) catch {\n                    skipped_count += 1;\n                    continue;\n                };\n                imported_count += 1;\n            }\n        } else {\n            // Replace mode: skip if exists\n            if (try store.exists(issue.id)) {\n                skipped_count += 1;\n                continue;\n            }\n            store.insert(issue) catch {\n                skipped_count += 1;\n                continue;\n            };\n            imported_count += 1;\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Single atomic save\n    if (!global.no_auto_flush) {\n        store.saveToFile() catch {\n            try common.outputErrorTyped(ImportResult, &output, structured_output, \"failed to save issues\");\n            return BatchError.StorageError;\n        };\n    }\n\n    // Output result\n    if (structured_output) {\n        try output.printJson(ImportResult{\n            .success = true,\n            .issues_imported = imported_count,\n            .issues_updated = if (import_args.merge) updated_count else null,\n            .issues_skipped = skipped_count + imported_issues.corruption_count,\n        });\n    } else if (!global.quiet) {\n        if (import_args.merge and updated_count > 0) {\n            try output.success(\"Imported {d}, updated {d}, skipped {d} issue(s)\", .{\n                imported_count,\n                updated_count,\n                skipped_count,\n            });\n        } else {\n            try output.success(\"Imported {d}, skipped {d} issue(s)\", .{ imported_count, skipped_count });\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/// Read file content into a buffer.\nfn readFileContent(path: []const u8, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) ![]u8 {\n    const file = try std.fs.cwd().openFile(path, .{});\n    defer file.close();\n    return try file.readToEndAlloc(allocator, 100 * 1024 * 1024); // 100MB max\n}\n\n/// Check if a file contains git merge conflict markers.\nfn hasMergeConflicts(path: []const u8, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) !bool {\n    const file = std.fs.cwd().openFile(path, .{}) catch |err| switch (err) {\n        error.FileNotFound => return false,\n        else => return err,\n    };\n    defer file.close();\n\n    const content = try file.readToEndAlloc(allocator, 1024 * 1024 * 10);\n    defer allocator.free(content);\n\n    const markers = [_][]const u8{ \"<<<<<<<\", \"=======\", \">>>>>>>\" };\n    for (markers) |marker| {\n        if (std.mem.indexOf(u8, content, marker) != null) return true;\n    }\n    return false;\n}\n\n/// Get the default actor name from environment.\nfn getDefaultActor() ?[]const u8 {\n    const builtin = @import(\"builtin\");\n    if (builtin.os.tag == .windows) return null;\n    return std.posix.getenv(\"USER\") orelse std.posix.getenv(\"USERNAME\");\n}\n\n/// Read the ID prefix from config.yaml, defaulting to \"bd\".\nfn getConfigPrefix(allocator: std.mem.Allocator, beads_dir: []const u8) ![]u8 {\n    const config_path = try std.fs.path.join(allocator, &.{ beads_dir, \"config.yaml\" });\n    defer allocator.free(config_path);\n\n    const file = std.fs.cwd().openFile(config_path, .{}) catch {\n        return try allocator.dupe(u8, \"bd\");\n    };\n    defer file.close();\n\n    const content = file.readToEndAlloc(allocator, 4096) catch {\n        return try allocator.dupe(u8, \"bd\");\n    };\n    defer allocator.free(content);\n\n    if (std.mem.indexOf(u8, content, \"prefix:\")) |prefix_pos| {\n        const after_prefix = content[prefix_pos + 7 ..];\n        var i: usize = 0;\n        while (i < after_prefix.len and (after_prefix[i] == ' ' or after_prefix[i] == '\\t')) {\n            i += 1;\n        }\n\n        if (i < after_prefix.len) {\n            if (after_prefix[i] == '\"') {\n                i += 1;\n                const start = i;\n                while (i < after_prefix.len and after_prefix[i] != '\"' and after_prefix[i] != '\\n') {\n                    i += 1;\n                }\n                if (i > start) {\n                    return try allocator.dupe(u8, after_prefix[start..i]);\n                }\n            } else {\n                const start = i;\n                while (i < after_prefix.len and after_prefix[i] != '\\n' and after_prefix[i] != ' ' and after_prefix[i] != '\\t') {\n                    i += 1;\n                }\n                if (i > start) {\n                    return try allocator.dupe(u8, after_prefix[start..i]);\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    return try allocator.dupe(u8, \"bd\");\n}\n\n// --- Tests ---\n\ntest \"BatchError enum exists\" {\n    const err: BatchError = BatchError.WorkspaceNotInitialized;\n    try std.testing.expect(err == BatchError.WorkspaceNotInitialized);\n}\n\ntest \"BatchResult struct works\" {\n    const result = BatchResult{\n        .success = true,\n        .issues_created = 5,\n    };\n    try std.testing.expect(result.success);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 5), result.issues_created.?);\n}\n\ntest \"ImportResult struct works\" {\n    const result = ImportResult{\n        .success = true,\n        .issues_imported = 10,\n        .issues_skipped = 2,\n    };\n    try std.testing.expect(result.success);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 10), result.issues_imported.?);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 2), result.issues_skipped.?);\n}\n\ntest \"runAddBatch detects uninitialized workspace\" {\n    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n\n    const batch_args = args.AddBatchArgs{};\n    const global = args.GlobalOptions{ .silent = true, .data_path = \"/nonexistent/path\" };\n\n    const result = runAddBatch(batch_args, global, allocator);\n    try std.testing.expectError(BatchError.WorkspaceNotInitialized, result);\n}\n\ntest \"runImport detects uninitialized workspace\" {\n    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n\n    const import_args = args.ImportArgs{ .file = \"test.jsonl\" };\n    const global = args.GlobalOptions{ .silent = true, .data_path = \"/nonexistent/path\" };\n\n    const result = runImport(import_args, global, allocator);\n    try std.testing.expectError(BatchError.WorkspaceNotInitialized, result);\n}\n\ntest \"hasMergeConflicts returns false for missing file\" {\n    const has_conflicts = try hasMergeConflicts(\"/nonexistent/path.jsonl\", std.testing.allocator);\n    try std.testing.expect(!has_conflicts);\n}\n\ntest \"hasMergeConflicts returns false for clean file\" {\n    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n    const test_dir = try test_util.createTestDir(allocator, \"batch_clean\");\n    defer allocator.free(test_dir);\n    defer test_util.cleanupTestDir(test_dir);\n\n    const test_path = try std.fs.path.join(allocator, &.{ test_dir, \"clean.jsonl\" });\n    defer allocator.free(test_path);\n\n    const file = try std.fs.cwd().createFile(test_path, .{});\n    try Add to ~/.bashrc: source <(bz completions bash)\n\n_bz_completions() {\n    local cur prev words cword\n    _init_completion || return\n\n    local commands=\"init create q show update close reopen delete list ready blocked search stale count dep label comments history audit sync config info stats doctor version schema completions\"\n\n    if [[ $cword -eq 1 ]]; then\n        COMPREPLY=($(compgen -W \"$commands\" -- \"$cur\"))\n        return\n    fi\n\n    case ${words[1]} in\n        show|update|close|reopen|delete|comments|history)\n            # Complete with issue IDs\n            local ids=$(bz list --quiet 2>/dev/null)\n            COMPREPLY=($(compgen -W \"$ids\" -- \"$cur\"))\n            ;;\n        dep)\n            if [[ $cword -eq 2 ]]; then\n                COMPREPLY=($(compgen -W \"add remove list tree cycles\" -- \"$cur\"))\n            else\n                local ids=$(bz list --quiet 2>/dev/null)\n                COMPREPLY=($(compgen -W \"$ids\" -- \"$cur\"))\n            fi\n            ;;\n        label)\n            if [[ $cword -eq 2 ]]; then\n                COMPREPLY=($(compgen -W \"add remove list list-all\" -- \"$cur\"))\n completions zsh)\n\n_bz() {\n    local -a commands\n    commands=(\n        'init:Initialize beads workspace'\n        'create:Create new issue'\n        'q:Quick capture (create + print ID only)'\n        'show:Display issue details'\n        'update:Update issue fields'\n        'close:Close an issue'\n        'reopen:Reopen a closed issue'\n        'delete:Soft delete (tombstone)'\n        'list:List issues with filters'\n        'ready:Show actionable issues (unblocked)'\n        'blocked:Show blocked issues'\n        'search:Full-text search'\n        'stale:Find stale issues'\n        'count:Count issues'\n        'dep:Manage dependencies'\n        'label:Manage labels'\n        'comments:Manage comments'\n        'history:Show issue history'\n        'audit:View audit log'\n        'sync:Sync with JSONL file'\n        'config:Manage configuration'\n        'info:Workspace info'\n        'stats:Project statistics'\n        'doctor:Run diagnostics'\n        'version:Show version'\n        'schema:View storage schema'\n        'completions:Generate shell completions'\n    )\n\n    local -a global_opts\n    global_opts=(\n        '--json[Output in JSON format]'\n        '--toon[Output in TOON format]'\n        '-q[Quiet mode]'\n        '--quiet[Quiet mode]'\n        '-v[Verbose mode]'\n        '--verbose[Verbose mode]'\n        '--no-color[Disable colors]'\n        '--data[Override .beads/ directory]:directory:_files -/'\n    )\n\n    _arguments -C \\\n        $global_opts \\\n        '1:command:->command' \\\n        '*::arg:->args'\n\n    case $state in\n        command)\n            _describe 'command' commands\n            ;;\n        args)\n            case ${words[1]} in\n                show|update|close|reopen|delete)\n                    _arguments label_cmds\n                    ;;\n                completions)\n                    local -a shells\n                    shells=('bash' 'zsh' 'fish' 'powershell')\n                    _describe
